COUNTIFS extends the <a href=\"/node/109\" style=\"line-height:20px;background-color:transparent;color:rgb(31, 79, 130);nodepath:/html/body/div[3]/div/div[2]/main/div/div/div/div/div/div[1]/div/div[3]/div/div/div/div/div[10]/div[2]/div/p/a[1];pagepos:245;cwidth:61;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:61px;wocalc:61px;hcalc:20;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:7;ez_min_text_wdth:58;req_px_area:2440;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20px;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;\" target=\"_blank\" eza=\"cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:61px;wocalc:61px;hcalc:20px;rend_px_area:0;\" cwidth=\"0\">COUNTIF</a> function which only allows one criteria. It is similar to <a href=\"/node/84\" style=\"line-height:20px;background-color:transparent;color:rgb(31, 79, 130);nodepath:/html/body/div[3]/div/div[2]/main/div/div/div/div/div/div[1]/div/div[3]/div/div/div/div/div[10]/div[2]/div/p/a[2];pagepos:247;cwidth:51;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:51px;wocalc:51px;hcalc:20;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:7;ez_min_text_wdth:49;req_px_area:2040;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20px;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;\" eza=\"cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:51px;wocalc:51px;hcalc:20px;rend_px_area:0;\" cwidth=\"0\">SUMIFS</a>, which will find the sum of all cells that match a set of multiple criteria. This lesson shows you how to use COUNTIFS and provides some practical examples to help you understand how it works.</p>\n</div>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-term-node-tid\"
